 The group of different planets, comets, meteors and other celestial bodies that revolve around the Sun is called the Solar System
 soramandal ke puure urja kaa strot surya hi he
 Important facts related to solar system are as follows: (1) There are 8 planets in the solar system - Mercury, Venus, Earth, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Arun and Varuna
 (2)soramandal main 9waan grah pluto tha, lekin vaigyanikon ne pluto ko grah kii shrenee se hataa diya kyonki yah bahut chota tha
 (3) There are also satellites of planets which orbit their planets
 (4)surya hamaari gallexi milky ve se lagbhag 30,000 prakaash varsh kii duuri par sthit he
 (5) The Sun is orbiting around the Milky Way at a speed of 250 km / s
 (6)milky ve ke chaaro ore ghoomane main laga vakt 25 karod varsh he, jise brahmad varsh bhi kehete hai
 (7) The Sun revolves on its axis from east to west
 (8)hamaara soramandal kareeb 4
 Came into existence 6 billion years ago
 (9)surya hamaari prithvi se 13 lakh guna bada he
 (10) The largest planet is Jupiter and the smallest planet is Mercury
 (11)surya kaa vyas 13 lakh 92 hajaar he kilometre he, or ye prithvi ke vyas se 110 guna zyada he
 (12) Mercury, Venus, Saturn, Jupiter and Mars These five planets can be seen with open eyes
 (13)shukr soramandal kaa sabase garm grah he
 (14) 71 percent hydrogen in the Sun, 26
 5 fisadi helium or 2
 5% are other elements
 (15)saura mandal main surya or khagoleey pind ek duusare se gurutvkarshan bal main bandhe hai
 (16) The Sun is the largest body of our solar system
 (17)soramandal main pindon ko teen shreniyon main baanta gaya he- paramparaagat grah, boune grah or laghu soramandaleey pind
 (18) The traditional planets are Mercury, Venus, Earth, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Uranus and Varuna
 (19)boune grahon main pluto, eries, seras, makemake, homia hai
 (20) Small solar atmospheric bodies include comets, satellites and other small celestial bodies
 (21)soramandal main bahut hi chote- chote arabon pind he jinhen dhoomaketu yaa puchchal taare kehete hai
 (22) Moon revolves around 6 planets and 3 dwarf planets

 Salman ended his work and reached Mumbai on Tuesday to take part in the court proceedings
 bollywood ke sabase popular actaramen se ek salmaan ke paas 2017 tak ke project hai or un par industry kaa 200 karod rupaya laga hua he
 Security linkages in court: Sources in the court said that the police has made preparations to tighten security in the court premises to prevent Salman's fans from entering the premises
 sutron ne bataaya ki adaalat ke bheetar keval mediakarmiyon, vakeelon or adaalat ke staff ko jane kii anumati hogi
 Judge DW Deshpande announced last month that he would deliver the verdict on 6 May
 unhone actor ko 6 may ko subah sava 11 baje adaalat main maujuud rahane ke liye saman bhi jari kiya tha
 The prosecution and defense debate in the case of 10 years may be completed on April 21
 magistrate kii ore se gaiyr iradatan hatya ke aarope shaamil karne or maamle ko satr adaalat ke paas bhejne ke baad bahes nai sire se hui thi
 a case of culpable homicide cannot be tried by a sessions court but by a magistrate and if found guilty, the offender can be punished for up to 10 years
 isse pehle magistrate salmaan ke khilaaf laaparvaahee se or tej gati se gaadi chalaane ke maamle main sunwaayee kar rahe the
 In this case, the accused can be punished up to two years under the IPC section
 driver kii gavaahi- main chalaa rahaa tha gadisalman (49) kaa kahana he ki vah durghatana ke samay gaadi nahin chalaa rahe the or us samay unka driver ashok singh gaadi chalaa rahaa tha
 Singh, appearing as a defense witness, has confirmed this
 haalanki pradeep gharaat ke netritv main abhiyojan paksh ne aarope lagaaya he ki salmaan ek baar se ‚Äòbacardi ram‚Äô pine ke baad gaadi chalaa rahe the jabaki actor kaa kahana he ki vah sharaab nahin balki pani pi rahe the
 Though the prosecution argued that apart from Salman, his police body guard Ravindra Patil and singer friend Kamal Khan were present in the car, but the actor argued that there was also a fourth person in the car, Ashok Singh
 ek adaalat ne 2013 main salmaan ke khilaaf ek taaja sunwaayee ke dauraan gaiyr iradatan hatya ke aarope tay kiye the
 The prosecution questioned 27 witnesses to prove their case
 sarkari kraine ne peediton par gira di thi SUV: salmaan ke vakilsalmaan ke vakil shrikant shivade ne tark diya ki mritak kii postmortem report bataati he ki uski maut kuchle jane se lagi choton se huin or ye chotein us samay lagi thim jab police kii ore se bulaai gai kraine baari esayuvi ko ek baar main nahin uthaa saki thi or usne ise peediton par gira diya tha
 The defense counsel argued that the car crashed into a shop as the left wheel exploded
 unka kahana tha ki durghatanasthal par dukaan ke paas sadak kii marammat ho rahi thi or us jagah par pathar bikhare pade the
 The prosecution said that it was basing the statement made by Patil to the police
 patil ne kaha tha ki usne abhinayta ko tej gati or laaparvaahee se vaahan na chalaane kii salaah di thi lekin salmaan ne uski baat par dhyaan nahin diya
 Patil died during the trial

 johnson ne do ke ausat se aath ran dekar do wicket bhi chatkaaye
